You may ask me any question your heart desires, but I shall share with you the higher purpose that awaits you all...\"</p><p>*This is where you should insert your adventure seeds, the conclusion of this adventure is the water spirit&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=29\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=29\">Alamera</a>&nbsp;giving them their next goal and mission and is meant to allow you to start your own adventure, or connect into another pre-written adventure.*&nbsp;</p><h3 style=\"text-align: center;\" data-mce-style=\"text-align: center;\">End of Adventure</h3><h1 style=\"text-align: center;\" data-mce-style=\"text-align: center;\">Thanks for playing! Hope you enjoyed it!</h1>"

Media that should be displayed will be clickable within these notes, or on the right side margin. All asset references will appear as links or on the left side margin, and can be interacted with similarly to asset cards. You can click media and images. Start this adventure off by showing your players this one<img src=\"https://www.gmforge.io/content/adventures/blessedwell/beginning.jpg\" width=\"189\" height=\"87\" data-mce-src=\"../content/adventures/blessedwell/beginning.jpg\">&nbsp;and reading the text below***</span></p><p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our Adventure begins as all great legends do, in a quiet town beautifully isolated from the conflicts of the world. The town is known as the Rosen Orchard and rests peacefully in the heart of a&nbsp;forest, fostering and nurturing a slow and humble existence. It provides for animals, and man alike, and its inhabitants are of the kindest of folk. Children roam the streets, laughing and playing, and the sweet chirping of birds and bugs provide a calming ambience to the town.</span></p><p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">There have recently been rumblings of the �blessed well� re-awaking and the Rosen Orchard has soon become a popular location for all, with pursuits of all kinds. As one might suspect the Rosen Orchard was not prepared to accommodate such an influx of visitors, but nonetheless the people of Rosen Orchard has extended their welcoming arms to all, for better or for worse. As there is not enough space within town, many adventures have resigned to setting up camp just outside the Rosen Orchard, where a mini shanty town of tents and tree-forts have arisen.</span></p><p>&nbsp;***<span class=\"mce-preview-object mce-object-iframe\" contenteditable=\"false\" data-mce-object=\"iframe\" data-mce-p-allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\" data-mce-p-src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/XEv0L6PRCnc\"><iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/XEv0L6PRCnc\" width=\"179\" height=\"100\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\" data-mce-src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/XEv0L6PRCnc\"></iframe><span class=\"mce-shim\"></span></span>&nbsp;Suggested Background music while players figure out what they want to do. Luther is a&nbsp;friendly eager boy***</span></p><p><br><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">***<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=16\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=16\">Bastion</a>&nbsp;is a young child, roughly 8 years of age and of similar physique as Luther, he has straight blonde hair cut short. He has a collection of bracelets and toys, but has a slingshot and a pouch of what can only be assumed to be rocks. He carries a stuffed bear as his backpack. Bastion is a chatty naive boy, kind hearted but behaves like a typical 8 year old</span>***</p><p>The day begins to wane, and you notice that people are flocking to the Rosen Orchard's tavern. People&nbsp;seem to be especially eager to get inside.&nbsp;</p><p>***Find a way to convince your group to all end up at the tavern***</p><p>Once inside you are greeted with the hustle and bustle of&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=19\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=19\">Nimbly</a>'s tavern.</p><p><img src=\"https://www.gmforge.io/content/adventures/blessedwell/tavern.jpg\" width=\"163\" height=\"113\" data-mce-src=\"../content/adventures/blessedwell/tavern.jpg\"></p><p>A little halfling is scampering around the tables, cheerfully attending to the many customers needs. It is clear this tavern wasn't prepared for this influx of visitors, but the Rosen Orchard's hospitality isn't easily dissuaded. Tables have been thrown together, groups of adventurers are tightly packed throughout the tavern and are all gregariously enjoying themselves.&nbsp;</p><p>***If your group has yet to come together, there are convieniently only a number of seats remaining that matches the group size (<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=17\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=17\">Luther</a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=16\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=16\">Bastion</a>&nbsp;can be added here too)***</p><p>***<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=19\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=19\">Nimbly</a>&nbsp;is an energetic halfling with an irish accent, his only concern is that all of his guests are enjoying themselves and feel welcomed into the Rosen Orchard's family***<br>Given the traffic you are suprised to see&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=19\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=19\">Nimbly</a>&nbsp;so attentive, he makes eye contact with your group and gingerly approaches.</p><p><a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=19\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=19\">Nimbly</a>&nbsp;says</p><p><a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=19\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=19\">Nimbly</a>&nbsp;: \"Tip of the even'n to ya laddies, what can I do' ye for? The rest of the night winds down smoothly, and uneventfully. Other adventurers slowly trickle out, and head off to the shanty town just outside the Rosen Orchard's perimeter.</p><p>*The shanty town is an opprotunity for you as the GM to get creative, if you want to allow some time for shopping, impromptu combat, or anything you could imagine the shanty town is a great place to do so.               "current": "<p>***This section contains descriptions of the several areas, each of them giving a different piece of the riddle&nbsp;<em><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">�Needeth are legends, when thy water floweth. And w</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">hen thy life trickles, it must be unleashed, only h</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">oly hands can embrace thine awakening, for l</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">ife is borne from baptism, but it shall be fleeting�</span></em>***</p><p>By now your group should have accomplished the following</p><ul><li>Gotten to know one another</li><li>Become a party</li><li>Met&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=19\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=19\">Nimbly</a>&nbsp;and discovered the secret to awakening the well is by collecting the riddles (4 in total)</li></ul><p>***The party can choose to split up and look for clues, or move as a unit from point to point. There are four areas that prove fruitful for the adventures. The Stables, The main street of the Rosen Orchard, the Church, and on the back of the statue in the Basin***</p><h2 style=\"margin: 0; font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;\" data-mce-style=\"margin: 0; font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;\">&nbsp;The Street Pastor</h2><hr class=\"h2\" style=\"display: block; outline: none; border: none; width: 100%; height: 1px; background: grey; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;\" data-mce-style=\"display: block; outline: none; border: none; width: 100%; height: 1px; background: grey; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;\"><p>In the main street of the Rosen Orchard there is a stone golem,&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=22\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=22\">Gondalath</a>, who is sharing one of the riddles. However,&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=22\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=22\">Gondalath</a>&nbsp;doesn't speak at the same pace as normal humans, he has a slower tempo to his speech, which requires the group to listen to him intently for several minutes to digest what he is saying. Should you need, you can cure him of his speech impediment with another adventurer, and have your group overhear what he is saying.</p><p>�Needeth are legends, when thy water floweth.�</p><p>&nbsp;<a href=\"|asset|=20\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=20\">Old man Jenkins</a>&nbsp;: \"Halt! Stop right there criminals!\"<br></p><p><img src=\"/content/adventures/blessedwell/stables.jpg\" width=\"570\" data-mce-src=\"../content/adventures/blessedwell/stables.jpg\"></p><h2 style=\"margin: 0; font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;\" data-mce-style=\"margin: 0; font-size: 1.4em; font-weight: bold;\">&nbsp;Blessed Well</h2><hr class=\"h2\" style=\"display: block; outline: none; border: none; width: 100%; height: 1px; background: grey; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;\" data-mce-style=\"display: block; outline: none; border: none; width: 100%; height: 1px; background: grey; margin-top: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;\"><p>&nbsp;The Blessed Well is a large empty lake that lies within walking distance of the Rosen Orchard. It is a massive lake, surrounded by a deep and steep ridge. This ridge can be traversed, but it is a difficult (but short) trek down. Once at the bottom, The Basin of the Blessed Well&nbsp;offers a level floor, that is riddled with cracks and mysterious pores. Upon further inspection the edges of the Basin have larger pores, similiar size to telephone poles.</p><p><em>The Fountain Ornament</em></p><p>In the center of the Basin there is large fountain ornament, that extends to the same height of the ridge. This ornament has a fountain piece at the top, but beneath the ridgeline is a very plain looking obelisk, and it is extermely difficult to climb. At the base of the centerpiece is a&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/content/adventures/blessedwell/statue.jpg\" data-mce-href=\"../content/adventures/blessedwell/statue.jpg\">statue of a woman</a>, hands clasped in a praying position. She appears to be made of solid stone, however she is implanted in a grooved area, allowing for a little bit of sliding in one horizontal direction away from the fountain ornament. Above the statue is a little grooved implant, where it seems something small can be placed, and above that is a circular hole that has a gentle stream of water trickling down to the basin's floor. The ornament has a piece of the riddle engraved on the face directly opposite to the face the statue is on.&nbsp;</p><p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">�And when thy life trickles, it must be unleashed�</span></p><p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\" data-mce-style=\"font-weight: 400;\">*Consider throwing a climbing test at your players to have them descend the ridge, you can also provide a rough trail, but the ridge should poise a threat of its own (not a lethal threat mind you). This is to deter the other 'npc' adventurering groups, and explains why no other group has found the riddle here*</span></p><h2><strong><a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/content/adventures/blessedwell/stables.jpg\" data-mce-href=\"../content/adventures/blessedwell/stables.jpg\">The Stables</a></strong></h2><p><a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=20\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=20\">Old man Jenkins</a>&nbsp;runs the stables of the Rosen Orchard, it is a humble stable that only has a couple of horses. Beyond the stable is a large pasture for sheep and cows to graze freely, gated by a simple wood fence.&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=20\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=20\">Old man Jenkins</a>&nbsp;takes great pride in what he does, even though many would find his duties demeaning or beneath them. He loves his work, is a gregarious&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=20\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=20\">old man</a>&nbsp;and seems almost incapable of anything but kindness. He will greet all who approach him, but in order for your group to knock his memory loose of&nbsp;a riddle, they will need to assist him in a half a days worth of hard labor, leaving them exhausted but revealing a piece of the riddle.</p><p>�only holy hands can embrace thine awakening�</p><p>***It is imperative to get your players to establish a good relationship with&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=20\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=20\">Old man Jenkins</a>, for he will be needed in convincing&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=21\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=21\">Father Michael</a>&nbsp;that the group is worthy enough to take one of the sacred relics of the Rosen Orchard to the Blessed Well***</p><h2><strong><a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/content/adventures/blessedwell/church.jpg\" data-mce-href=\"../content/adventures/blessedwell/church.jpg\">The Church</a></strong></h2><p><a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=21\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=21\">Father Michael</a>&nbsp;is the church's pastor, and he is a hard beaten fellow, who comes off as a curt and stern. He is devoute beyond reason, but still maintains a healthy level of understanding for other beliefs. He worships the god of nature, and is in high demand. Adventurers must stand in a line, or find an alternate way to meet with&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.gmforge.io/session/%7Casset%7C=21\" data-mce-href=\"|asset|=21\">Father Michael</a>, for all adventuring groups are trying to gain his audience. Once inside they are not guarenteed to convince him to share his information, and can only do so by showing the utmost respect for the god of nature and the church.
